Paying Zakat Early: Permissibility and Proof
Ruling with proof on permissibility of early zakat payment

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi ruling on paying zakat before the year and explain the proof from the hadith of al-Abbas.

Core Idea
You can pay zakat early once you own the nisab—the year is not a condition for payment.

Many students assume that zakat can only be paid after a full lunar year. However, the Hanafi school teaches that once you own the minimum nisab, you may discharge your zakat early. This lesson examines the ruling and its evidence from the hadith of al-Abbas, clarifying the legal reasoning behind it.

Guided Path
1
Identify the act and its legal context
The act is paying zakat before the completion of one lunar year (ta'jil al-zakat). The context is a person who owns the nisab but the year has not yet passed.
Zakat is an annual obligation on specific wealth.
2
State the Hanafi ruling
The Hanafi ruling is that it is permissible (ja'iz) and valid; the zakat is discharged and does not need to be repeated.
This is from Zahir al-Riwayah.
3
Identify the effective cause (sabab)
The nisab (minimum wealth) is the original cause for zakat obligation. Once the cause exists, payment is valid even before the year ends.
The year is not a condition but a timeframe for collection.
4
Analyze the hadith proof
The hadith states that al-Abbas asked the Prophet about giving charity (zakat) before it becomes due, and the Prophet granted him a concession. This indicates permissibility.
The phrase 'farrakhasa' (granted concession) implies permission in Hanafi usul.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
الشرح الثميرى الجزء الاوّل)
كتاب الزكوة
یعنی ایک آدمی نصاب کا مالک ہے لیکن اس نصاب پر سال نہیں گزرا ہے اور وہ ابھی زکوۃ ادا کر دینا چاہتا ہے تو جائز ہے۔ زکوۃ ادا ہو جائیگی۔
مال نصاب اصل سبب ہے اور وہ پایا گیا تو گویا کہ سبب پایا گیا اس لئے زکوۃ کی ادائیگی ہو جائیگی (۲) حدیث میں ہے عن علي ان العباس سأل النبي صلى الله عليه وسلم في تعجيل الصدقة قبل ان تحل فرخص له في ذلك (الف) (ابوداؤد شریف، باب فی تجمیل الزکوة ص ۲۳۶ نمبر ۶۲۴ ارترمذی شریف، باب ما جاء فی تجمیل الزکوۃ ص ۱۴۶ نمبر ۶۷۸) اس حدیث سے معلوم ہوا کہ سال گزرنے سے پہلے زکوۃ ادا کر سکتا ہے کیونکہ حضرت عباس کو اس کی اجازت دی تھی۔
حاشیہ : (الف) حضرت عباس نے حضور سے زکوۃ جلدی دینے کے بارے میں پوچھا وقت آنے سے پہلے تو آپ نے اس بارے میں رخصت دیدی۔
Al-Sharh al-Thamiri, Part One. Book of Zakat. Meaning, a person owns the nisab but a year has not passed over this nisab, and he wishes to pay zakat now, then it is permissible. Zakat will be discharged. The wealth (nisab) is the original cause, and when it is found, it is as if the cause is found, therefore payment of zakat will be valid. (2) There is a hadith: From Ali that al-Abbas asked the Prophet (peace be upon him) about hastening charity before it becomes due, and he granted him a concession for that. (Abu Dawud, chapter on hastening zakat, p. 236 no. 624; Tirmidhi, chapter on hastening zakat, p. 146 no. 678). From this hadith it is understood that one can pay zakat before the year passes because the Prophet granted permission to al-Abbas. Marginal note: (a) Al-Abbas asked the Prophet about paying zakat early, before the time, and he gave permission in this regard.
Source pages p. 321

Commentary
This is a ruling with proof passage. The author explains the permissibility of paying zakat before the completion of one lunar year (al-hawl). The key principle is that the nisab (minimum threshold of wealth) is the effective cause (sabab) for zakat obligation. Since the cause is present, paying zakat early is valid and the payment discharges the obligation. The author cites the hadith of al-Abbas (may Allah be pleased with him) who asked the Prophet (peace be upon him) about paying charity (zakat) before it becomes due, and the Prophet granted permission. This hadith is recorded by Abu Dawud and al-Tirmidhi. The marginal note clarifies that the permission was specifically for paying early. This ruling is established in the Hanafi school: it is permissible to pay zakat in advance once the nisab is possessed, even if the year has not yet passed. However, if one pays before possessing the nisab, it is not valid. The Hanafi school relies on this proof (dalil) and also on reasoning (qiyas): since zakat is an act of worship that can be performed immediately after the cause, advancing it is analogous to other acts allowed before their complete time.

Key Terms
تعجيل (ta'jīl): Hastening or advancing the payment of zakat before the completion of the lunar year.
نصاب (niṣāb): The minimum amount of wealth that triggers the obligation of zakat.
زكاة (zakāh): The obligatory charity on specific types of wealth at specific rates after a lunar year.

Zakat on Silver: Nisab, Rate, and Inclusion of Jewelry
Rulings on nisab and rate of zakat on silver with proofs.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the nisab of silver (200 dirhams), calculate zakat at 2.5% with the 40-dirham increment rule, and explain the Hanafi position that zakat applies to silver jewelry and vessels.

Core Idea
Silver's nisab is 200 dirhams (2.5% due); additional zakat requires 40-dirham increments; jewelry is included.

This lesson presents the foundational Hanafi rulings on zakat of silver. It covers the nisab threshold, the standard rate, the unique increment rule for amounts exceeding 200 dirhams, and the Hanafi inclusion of silver jewelry and vessels. The proofs from hadith are cited, including the famous hadith of Abu Sa'id al-Khudri and Mu'adh ibn Jabal.

Guided Path
1
Identify the nisab and rate
The matn states no zakat below 200 dirhams; at exactly 200 dirhams, 5 dirhams are due (2.5%). Confirm with the hadith of five uqiyah (each uqiyah = 40 dirhams).
Nisab: 200 dirhams; rate: 2.5%.
2
Understand the increment rule
For amounts above 200 dirhams, no zakat is due until the excess reaches 40 dirhams. Then, for every 40 dirhams, 1 dirham is due. This is the position of Abu Hanifah based on the hadith of Mu'adh.
Example: 240 dirhams = 5 (for 200) + 1 (for 40) = 6 dirhams.
3
Note the scope of 'fiddah'
The commentary clarifies that 'fiddah' includes not only dirham coins but also silver jewelry and vessels. Hanafis include these based on the hadith of the woman with gold bracelets, by analogy (qiyas).
Shafi'is and Malikis may exempt jewelry, but Hanafis oblige zakat.
4
Apply the ruling
Calculate zakat for a given amount: first, check if nisab (200 dirhams) is met. If so, calculate 2.5% on the base 200, then add 1 dirham for each full 40-dirham increment above 200.
Remember: partial increments (<40) are ignored.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
باب زكوة الفضة
۱۳۸۹ (۱) ليس فيما دون مائتى درهم صدقة فاذا كانت مائتى درهم وحال عليها الحول ففيها خمسة دراهم [۴۹۰] (۲) ولا شيء فى الزيادة حتى تبلغ اربعين درهما فيكون فيها در هم ثم في كل اربعین درهمادرهم عند ابي حنيفة.
ضروری نوٹ فضہ کے معنی چاندی کے ہیں۔ یہاں فضہ سے مراد درہم، چاندی کا زیور اور چاندی کا برتن مراد ہے۔ حنفیہ کے نزدیک ان ساری چیزوں میں زکوۃ ہے۔ دلیل یہ حدیث ہے ان امراة اتت رسول الله و معها ابنة لها وفي يد ابنتها مسكتان غليظتان من ذهب فقال اتعطين زكوة هذا؟ قالت لا قال ايسرك ان يسورك الله بهما يوم القيامة سوارين من نار؟ قال فخلعتهما والقتهما الى النبي الا الله وقالت هما لله ورسوله (الف) (ابوداود شریف، باب الکنز ما هووز کوۃ المحلی ص ۲۲۵ نمبر ۱۵۶۳) اس حدیث سے معلوم ہوا کہ زیور کی بھی زکوۃ لازم ہے۔
[۴۹۰] (۱) دوسو درہم سے کم میں زکوۃ نہیں ہے، پس جب کہ دو سو درہم ہو جائے اور اس پر سال گزر جائے تو اس میں پانچ درہم ہے۔ حدیث میں موجود ہے کہ دو سو درہم سے کم میں زکوۃ نہیں ہے۔ سمعت ابا سعيد الخدري قال قال رسول الله ليس فيما دون خمس ذود صدقة من الابل و ليس فيما دون خمس اواق صدقة (ب) ( بخاری شریف ، باب زکوۃ الورق ص۱۹۴ نمبر ۱۴۴۷ر ابوداؤد شریف، نمبر ۱۵۷۲) اس حدیث سے معلوم ہوا کہ دو سو درہم سے کم میں زکوۃ نہیں ہے۔ اس لئے کہ ایک اوقیہ چالیس درہم کا ہوتا ہے تو پانچ اوقیہ دوسو درہم کے ہوں گے۔
[۴۹۰] (۲) پھر دو سو درہم سے زیادہ میں کچھ نہیں ہے یہاں تک کہ چالیس درہم ہو جائے ، پس چالیس درہم میں ایک درہم ہے۔ پھر ہر چالیس درہم میں ایک درہم ہے امام ابو حنیفہ کے نزدیک ۔ امام ابوحنیفہ کے نزدیک دو سودرہم کے بعد اس وقت تک کچھ لازم نہیں ہو گا جب تک کہ چالیس درہم نہ ہو جائے، البتہ چالیس درہم ہو جائے تو پھر اس میں ایک درہم لا زم ہوگا ۔۔ ان کی دلیل یہ حدیث ہے عن معاذ ان رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم امره حين وجهه الى اليمن ان لا تأخذ من الكسر شيئا اذا كانت الورق مائتى درهم فخذ منها خمسة دراهم، ولا تأخذ مما زاد شيئا حتى تبلغ اربعين درهما، واذا بلغ اربعين حاشیہ : (الف) ایک عورت آئی رسول اللہ کے پاس اور اس کے ساتھ ایک بچی تھی اور اس کی بچی کے ہاتھ پر سونے کے دو موٹے موٹے کنگن تھے تو آپ نے فرمایا کیا اس کی زکوۃ ادا کرتی ہو؟ کہنے لگی نہیں۔ آپ نے فرمایا کیا یہ تم کو اچھا لگے گا کہ اللہ اس کی وجہ سے دو آگ کے کنگن پہنائے۔ راوی فرماتے ہیں کہ اس عورت نے دونوں کنگنوں کو کھولا اور حضور کے سامنے ڈال دیا اور کہنے لگی یہ منگن اللہ اور اس کے رسول کے لئے ہیں (الف) آپ نے فرمایا پانچ اونٹ سے کم میں زکوۃ نہیں ہے اور پانچ اوقیہ چاندی سے کم میں زکوۃ نہیں ہے۔
Chapter on Zakat of Silver
1389 (1) There is no charity on less than two hundred dirhams. So when it reaches two hundred dirhams and a year passes over them, then five dirhams are due. [490] (2) And nothing is due on the increase until it reaches forty dirhams, then one dirham is due, then each forty dirhams one dirham, according to Abu Hanifah.
Necessary Note: Fiddah means silver. Here fiddah refers to dirhams, silver jewelry, and silver vessels. According to the Hanafis, zakat is due on all these items. The proof is this hadith: A woman came to the Messenger of Allah with her daughter, and on the hand of her daughter were two thick gold bracelets. He said, 'Do you give zakat on these?' She said, 'No.' He said, 'Would it please you that Allah should make you wear two bracelets of fire on the Day of Resurrection?' He (the narrator) said: She took them off and threw them to the Prophet saying, 'They are for Allah and His Messenger.' (A) (Abu Dawud, chapter on treasure and zakat on jewelry, p. 225 no. 1563). From this hadith it is understood that zakat is obligatory on jewelry as well.
[490] (1) There is no zakat on less than two hundred dirhams. So when it becomes two hundred dirhams and a year passes, then five dirhams are due. There is a hadith: I heard Abu Sa'id al-Khudri say: The Messenger of Allah said: 'There is no charity on less than five dhoud of camels, and there is no charity on less than five uqiyah (of silver).' (B) (Bukhari, chapter on zakat of waraq, p. 194 no. 1447; Abu Dawud, no. 1572). From this hadith it is understood that there is no zakat on less than two hundred dirhams, because one uqiyah is forty dirhams, so five uqiyah make two hundred dirhams.
[490] (2) Then nothing is due on the increase until it reaches forty dirhams; then one dirham is due. Then for every forty dirhams, one dirham, according to Abu Hanifah. According to Abu Hanifah, after two hundred dirhams, nothing is due until it reaches forty dirhams; but when it reaches forty dirhams, then one dirham is obligatory. His proof is the hadith from Mu'adh that the Messenger of Allah, when he sent him to Yemen, commanded him: 'Do not take anything from the surplus. When the silver reaches two hundred dirhams, take five dirhams from it, and do not take anything from what exceeds it until it reaches forty dirhams; and when it reaches forty...' Marginal note: (A) A woman came to the Messenger of Allah... (B) The Prophet said: 'There is no charity on less than five camels, and no charity on less than five uqiyah of silver.'
Source pages p. 322

Commentary
This passage presents the rulings (matn) on zakat of silver (fiddah) along with commentary. The first ruling: No zakat on silver below 200 dirhams. When one possesses exactly 200 dirhams for a full lunar year, zakat is 5 dirhams (2.5% of 200). This is based on the hadith of Abu Sa'id al-Khudri who reported the Prophet (peace be upon him) saying: 'There is no sadaqah (zakat) on less than five awsuq of camels, and no sadaqah on less than five uqiyah of silver.' One uqiyah equals 40 dirhams, so five uqiyah equal 200 dirhams. Thus, 200 dirhams is the nisab. The second ruling: For amounts above 200 dirhams, no zakat is due until the excess reaches 40 dirhams. When the total reaches 240 dirhams (i.e., 200 + 40), zakat is 6 dirhams (5 for the first 200, 1 for the 40). Thereafter, for every additional 40 dirhams, one dirham is due. This is the position of Imam Abu Hanifah. The author provides the hadith of Mu'adh ibn Jabal (may Allah be pleased with him) as proof. In that hadith, the Prophet instructed Mu'adh: when silver reaches 200 dirhams, take 5 dirhams; for any increase, take nothing until it reaches 40 dirhams, then take one dirham. The necessary note clarifies that 'fiddah' includes not only dirham coins but also silver jewelry and vessels, and zakat is due on them according to the Hanafi school, supported by the hadith of the woman with gold bracelets. This establishes that zakat applies to silver items used as ornaments.

Key Terms
فضة (fiḍḍah): Silver; in this context, silver coins (dirhams), silver jewelry, and silver vessels, all subject to zakat according to Hanafis.
درهم (dirham): A silver coin used as the standard unit for nisab; 200 dirhams is the nisab for silver.
اوقية (ūqiyyah): A unit of weight; 1 uqiyah = 40 dirhams. Used in the hadith to set the nisab at 5 uqiyah = 200 dirhams.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to Imam Abu Hanifah, how much zakat is due on 280 dirhams of silver held for one year?
A) 7 dirhams
B) 8 dirhams
C) 5 dirhams
D) 6 dirhams

Key Takeaway
Zakat on silver is 2.5% of the nisab (200 dirhams) with a 40-dirham increment rule; the Hanafi school includes all forms of silver, including jewelry and vessels.

Zakat — Almsgiving
beginner
6 min
Nisab of Silver and Abu Hanifa's Rule on Increments
States nisab, rate, and Abu Hanifa's exemption for increments below 40 dirhams

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the nisab of silver, the zakat rate, and explain Abu Hanifa's rule regarding increments below 40 dirhams.

Core Idea
Silver zakat begins at 200 dirhams; increments below 40 are exempt according to Abu Hanifa.

In this passage from the Book of Zakat, we learn the foundational rule for zakat on silver: a minimum threshold of 200 dirhams, with a 2.5% rate. But what happens when you have more than 200? Imam Abu Hanifa, relying on a specific hadith, ruled that no zakat is due on any amount until the excess reaches a full 40 dirhams. This lesson unpacks that ruling and its textual basis.

Guided Path
1
Identify the nisab and rate
Find the exact numbers: the nisab is 200 dirhams, and the zakat due is 5 dirhams (2.5%).
2
Locate the hadith evidence
Two hadith are cited: one from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri establishing the nisab, and one from Mu'adh ibn Jabal detailing the rule on increments.
The Mu'adh hadith is the key for the increment exemption.
3
Understand Abu Hanifa's rule
No zakat is due on any increase until it totals 40 dirhams. For example, 30 dirhams extra is exempt.
4
Explore the rationale
The hadith says 'do not take anything from the increase until it reaches forty dirhams.' This is the direct basis for Abu Hanifa's position.
The imperative 'fakhudh' indicates obligation, but the exemption is explicit.

الشرح الثميرى الجزء الاوّل) ۳۱۷ كتاب الزكوة باب زكوة الفضة ۱۳۸۹ (۱) ليس فيما دون مائتى درهم صدقة فاذا كانت مائتى درهم وحال عليها الحول ففيها خمسة دراهم [۴۹۰] (۲) ولا شيء فى الزيادة حتى تبلغ اربعين درهما فيكون فيها در هم ثم في كل اربعین درهمادرهم عند ابي حنيفة. باب زكوة الفضة كم ضروری نوٹ فضہ کے معنی چاندی کے ہیں۔ یہاں فضہ سے مراد درہم، چاندی کا زیور اور چاندی کا برتن مراد ہے۔ حنفیہ کے نزدیک ان ساری چیزوں میں زکوۃ ہے۔ دلیل یہ حدیث ہے ان امراة اتت رسول الله و معها ابنة لها وفي يد ابنتها مسكتان غليظتان من ذهب فقال اتعطين زكوة هذا؟ قالت لا قال ايسرك ان يسورك الله بهما يوم القيامة سوارين من نار؟ قال فخلعتهما والقتهما الى النبي الا الله وقالت هما لله ورسوله (الف) (ابوداود شریف، باب الکنز ما هووز کوۃ المحلی ص ۲۲۵ نمبر ۱۵۶۳) اس حدیث سے معلوم ہوا کہ زیور کی بھی زکوۃ لازم ہے۔ ۳۸۹] (۱) دوسو درہم سے کم میں زکوۃ نہیں ہے، پس جب کہ دو سو درہم ہو جائے اور اس پر سال گزر جائے تو اس میں پانچ درہم ہے۔ حدیث میں موجود ہے کہ دو سو درہم سے کم میں زکوۃ نہیں ہے۔ سم سمعت ابا سعید الخدري قال قال رسول الله ليس فيما دون خمس زود صدقة من الابل و ليس فيما دون خمس اواق صدقة (ب) ( بخاری شریف ، باب زکوۃ الورق ص۱۹۴ نمبر ۱۴۴۷ر ابوداؤد شریف، نمبر ۱۵۷۲) اس حدیث سے معلوم ہوا کہ دو سو درہم سے کم میں زکوۃ نہیں ہے۔ اس لئے کہ ایک اوقیہ چالیس درہم کا ہوتا ہے تو پانچ اوقیہ دوسو درہم کے ہوں گے۔ [۴۹۰] (۲) پھر دو سو درہم سے زیادہ میں کچھ نہیں ہے یہاں تک کہ چالیس درہم ہو جائے ، پس چالیس درہم میں ایک درہم ہے۔ پھر ہر چالیس درہم میں ایک درہم ہے امام ابو حنیفہ کے نزدیک ۔ امام ابوحنیفہ کے نزدیک دو سودرہم کے بعد اس وقت تک کچھ لازم نہیں ہو گا جب تک کہ چالیس درہم نہ ہو جائے، البتہ چالیس درہم ہو جائے تو پھر اس میں ایک درہم لا زم ہوگا ۔۔ ان کی دلیل یہ حدیث ہے عن معاذ ان رسول الله لا لا لا له امره حين وجهه الى اليمن ان لا تأخذ من الكسر شيئا اذا كانت الورق مائتى درهم فخذ منها خمسة دراهم، ولا تأخذ مما زاد شيئا حتى تبلغ اربعين درهما، واذا بلغ اربعين حاشیہ : (الف) ایک عورت آئی رسول اللہ کے پاس اور اس کے ساتھ ایک بچی تھی اور اس کی بچی کے ہاتھ پر سونے کے دو موٹے موٹے کنگن تھے تو آپ نے فرمایا کیا اس کی زکوۃ ادا کرتی ہو؟ کہنے لگی نہیں۔ آپ نے فرمایا کیا یہ تم کو اچھا لگے گا کہ اللہ اس کی وجہ سے دو آگ کے کنگن پہنائے۔ راوی فرماتے ہیں کہ اس عورت نے دونوں کنگنوں کو کھولا اور حضور کے سامنے ڈال دیا اور کہنے لگی یہ منگن اللہ اور اس کے رسول کے لئے ہیں (الف) آپ نے فرمایا پانچ اونٹ سے کم میں زکوۃ نہیں ہے اور پانچ اوقیہ چاندی سے کم میں زکوۃ نہیں ہے۔
The Sharh al-Thamiri, Part One, p. 317. Book of Zakat. Chapter on Zakat of Silver. (1) There is no sadaqah (zakat) on less than two hundred dirhams. When they are two hundred dirhams and a year passes, then five dirhams are due. [490] (2) And nothing is due on the increase until it reaches forty dirhams, then one dirham is due, then for every forty dirhams, one dirham, according to Abu Hanifa. Chapter of Zakat of Silver: Important note: The meaning of 'al-fidda' is silver. Here by 'fidda' is meant dirhams, silver jewelry, and silver vessels. According to the Hanafis, zakat is obligatory on all these. The evidence is the hadith: 'A woman came to the Messenger of Allah with her daughter, and on the daughter's hand were two thick bracelets of gold. He said: Do you give zakat on this? She said: No. He said: Would it please you that Allah should adorn you with two bracelets of fire on the Day of Resurrection? The narrator said: She removed them and threw them to the Prophet, saying: They are for Allah and His Messenger. (a) (Abu Dawud, Bab al-Kanz, etc.) From this hadith it is understood that zakat is obligatory on jewelry. (1) There is no zakat on less than two hundred dirhams. When it becomes two hundred dirhams and a year passes, then five dirhams are due. It is found in hadith that there is no zakat on less than two hundred dirhams. Sima' heard Abu Sa'id al-Khudri say: The Messenger of Allah said: There is no sadaqah on less than five camels, and there is no sadaqah on less than five uqiyah. (b) (Bukhari, Bab Zakat al-Waraq, etc.) From this hadith it is understood that there is no zakat on less than two hundred dirhams, because one uqiyah is forty dirhams, so five uqiyah are two hundred dirhams. [490] (2) Then nothing is due on more than two hundred dirhams until it reaches forty dirhams. Then for forty dirhams, one dirham is due. Then for every forty dirhams, one dirham, according to Abu Hanifa. According to Abu Hanifa, after two hundred dirhams, nothing is obligatory until it reaches forty dirhams. When it reaches forty dirhams, then one dirham is obligatory. His evidence is the hadith from Mu'adh: The Messenger of Allah, when he sent him to Yemen, ordered him not to take anything from the fraction (kisr). When the silver (waraq) reaches two hundred dirhams, take five dirhams from them, and do not take anything from the increase until it reaches forty dirhams. When it reaches forty, then take one dirham. (a) Footnote: A woman came to the Messenger of Allah with her daughter... (as above). The Prophet said: There is no zakat on less than five camels and no zakat on less than five uqiyah of silver.
Source pages p. 322

Commentary
This passage is a ruling statement with proof from the Book of Zakat, specifically the chapter on Zakat of Silver. It establishes the nisab (minimum threshold) for silver as 200 dirhams (approximately 595 grams of silver in modern terms). The rate is 2.5% (five dirhams on two hundred). The second part addresses the rule for increments above the nisab according to Imam Abu Hanifa: no zakat is due on any amount between 200 and 239 dirhams (since zakat only becomes due when the excess reaches a full 40 dirhams). For example, if one has 230 dirhams, only the base 200 dirhams are zakatable (5 dirhams), and the extra 30 dirhams are exempt from zakat. This is based on the hadith of Mu'adh ibn Jabal where the Prophet instructed not to take from the 'kisr' (fraction) until it reaches 40 dirhams. The Urdu commentary expands by including the hadith about jewelry to show that all forms of silver wealth are subject to zakat. The text also clarifies that 'fidda' includes dirhams (coins), jewelry, and vessels. This ruling is from the Zahir al-Riwayah and is the position of Abu Hanifa. The Sahibayn differ, as will be seen in the next passage.

Key Terms
درهم (dirham): A silver coin weighing approximately 2.975 grams; used as the standard measure for zakat on silver.
نصاب (nisab): The minimum amount of wealth that triggers the obligation of zakat.
كسور (kusur): Fractions or increments between the nisab and the next full nisab increment (40 dirhams).

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the passage, what is the nisab for silver, and what is the zakat amount due on it?
A) 100 dirhams, 2.5 dirhams
B) 200 dirhams, 5 dirhams
C) 40 dirhams, 1 dirham
D) 200 dirhams, 10 dirhams

Key Takeaway
Zakat on silver is obligatory when you possess 200 dirhams for a full lunar year, and according to Abu Hanifa, increments below 40 dirhams are exempt from zakat.
